Group Gamee:
    if system_object.Every(0.5):
        gamee_c2.66.gameeActionUpdateScore(Score, #0)

        gamee_c2.66.gameeActionGameInit(#0)
        gamee_c2.66.gameeActionGameReady
        system_object.SetVar(Game_Start, 1)

        system_object.SetVar(Show_Video, 0)
        system_object.SetVar(Video_Watched, 0)
        system_object.SetVar(Game_Over_Time, 0)
        system_object.SetVar(Lost, 0)
        if system_object.CompareVar(Start, =, 0):
            if Sprite.0.CompareInstanceVar($0, =, 1):
                Sprite.0.Destroy

        system_object.RestartLayout
        system_object.SetVar(Score, 0)
        system_object.SetVar(Start, 0)
        gamee_c2.66.gameeActionUpdateScore(Score, #0)
        system_object.SetVar(Check_Red_Spawn, 0)

        system_object.SetTimescale(0)
        Audio.52.Stop("bg")

        system_object.SetTimescale(1)

Group SaveState:
    if gamee_c2.66.gameeEventOnInitialized:
        gamee_c2.66.gameeActionRequestPlayerData
        if system_object.Compare(system_object.trim(gamee_c2.gameeSaveState), !=, ""):
            Rex_Hash.67.StringToHashTable(gamee_c2.gameeSaveState)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Coins"):
                system_object.SetVar(Coins, Rex_Hash.At("data.Coins"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(COINS_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Coins, Rex_Hash.At(COINS_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(COINS_KEY, 0)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Pet"):
                system_object.SetVar(Pet, Rex_Hash.At("data.Pet"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(PET_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Pet, Rex_Hash.At(PET_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(PET_KEY, 0)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Unlock_Pet_1"):
                system_object.SetVar(Unlock_Pet_1, Rex_Hash.At("data.Unlock_Pet_1"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(UNLOCK_PET_1_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Unlock_Pet_1, Rex_Hash.At(UNLOCK_PET_1_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(UNLOCK_PET_1_KEY, 0)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Unlock_Pet_2"):
                system_object.SetVar(Unlock_Pet_2, Rex_Hash.At("data.Unlock_Pet_2"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(UNLOCK_PET_2_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Unlock_Pet_2, Rex_Hash.At(UNLOCK_PET_2_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(UNLOCK_PET_2_KEY, 0)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Unlock_Pet_3"):
                system_object.SetVar(Unlock_Pet_3, Rex_Hash.At("data.Unlock_Pet_3"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(UNLOCK_PET_3_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Unlock_Pet_3, Rex_Hash.At(UNLOCK_PET_3_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(UNLOCK_PET_3_KEY, 0)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Ball_Speed"):
                system_object.SetVar(Ball_Speed, Rex_Hash.At("data.Ball_Speed"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(BALLSPEED_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Ball_Speed, Rex_Hash.At(BALLSPEED_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(BALLSPEED_KEY, 0.2)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Pet_Ball_Speed"):
                system_object.SetVar(Pet_Ball_Speed, Rex_Hash.At("data.Pet_Ball_Speed"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(PET_BALLSPEED_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Pet_Ball_Speed, Rex_Hash.At(PET_BALLSPEED_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(PET_BALLSPEED_KEY, 0.2)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Guns"):
                system_object.SetVar(Guns, Rex_Hash.At("data.Guns"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(GUNS_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Guns, Rex_Hash.At(GUNS_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(GUNS_KEY, 1)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Add_Ball_HP"):
                system_object.SetVar(Add_Ball_HP, Rex_Hash.At("data.Add_Ball_HP"))
            elif Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(ADD_BALLHP_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Add_Ball_HP, Rex_Hash.At(ADD_BALLHP_KEY))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(ADD_BALLHP_KEY, 0)
            if Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists("data.Damage"):
                system_object.SetVar(Damage, Rex_Hash.At("data.Damage"))
                if True:
                    system_object.SetVar(Damage_Price, (100 + (Damage * 50)))
            if system_object.Else and Rex_Hash.67.KeyExists(DAMAGE_KEY):
                system_object.SetVar(Damage, Rex_Hash.At(DAMAGE_KEY))
                if True:
                    system_object.SetVar(Damage_Price, (100 + (Damage * 50)))
            else:
                Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(DAMAGE_KEY, 1)
        else:
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(COINS_KEY, 0)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(PET_KEY, 0)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(UNLOCK_PET_1_KEY, 0)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(UNLOCK_PET_2_KEY, 0)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(UNLOCK_PET_3_KEY, 0)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(BALLSPEED_KEY, 0.2)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(PET_BALLSPEED_KEY, 0.2)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(GUNS_KEY, 1)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(ADD_BALLHP_KEY, 0)
            Rex_Hash.67.SetValueByKeyString(DAMAGE_KEY, 1)
